 Political background Elections to this seat have been held since 1952, but this Lok Sabha constituency was named Brahmapur in 1977
 1952 main yaha se uma charan patnayak chunaav jite
 Then the name of this seat was Ghumsur
 1952 main hi yahaan upachunaav kii naubat aa gai is baar sipiai ke bijay chandra das chunaav jite
 In 1957 the name of this seat became Ganjam
 is baar chunaav main bataur nirdaleey uma charan patnayak vijayi rahe

 is baar yahaan congress candidet kaa danka baja
